<TRIAL_NAME>
Welcome to the Open-Air Water Power Museum
</TRIAL_NAME>
<TRIAL_TYPE>
5
</TRIAL_TYPE>
<TRIAL_DESCRIPTION>
Welcome to the Open-Air Water Power Museum of the Piraeus Bank Group’s Cultural Foundation, in Dimitsana. Discover the Museum through 11 questions that challenge your knowledge and keen eye.During the game, questions will appear. Each of them may be answered with the help of a text, an object or a space in the Museum. In order to answer, you will be asked to go through some tasks (e.g. scan a QR code, type a keyword or a number, take a photo). But do not be in a hurry, all in time ... here time is going slower, in contrast to the flowing waters.Good luck with your quest!
</TRIAL_DESCRIPTION>

<TRIAL>
TRIAL

<TRIAL_ID>
2
</TRIAL_ID>
<TRIAL_NAME>
You are in Dimitsana
</TRIAL_NAME>
<TRIAL_TYPE>
5
</TRIAL_TYPE>
<TRIAL_DESCRIPTION>
You are in Dimitsana at the beginning of 1821. Your destiny and choices have led you to this mountainous village of Arcadia. Far from your beloved Mani. A misunderstanding during your engagement has forced you to leave your place hunted.Somewhere along the way, you heard that a great uprising is being prepared. Your father told you that in Dimitsana they are making the best gunpowder in all of Moria. Arriving at Dimitsana, the houses unfold on the rocks in front of your eyes at the side of the main road. You ask around and people tell you to head towards Kefalari of Ai Giannis just outside Dimitsana. There, in the powder mills they ask for labourers.
</TRIAL_DESCRIPTION>

TRIAL

<TRIAL_ID>

</TRIAL_ID>
<TRIAL_NAME>
Takes advantage of the power that water
</TRIAL_NAME>
<TRIAL_TYPE>
5
</TRIAL_TYPE>
<TRIAL_DESCRIPTION>
This simple installation takes advantage of the power that water gets while falling from a great hight, through the headrace, and as it rotates with force in the tub. They were used to process woolen goods at the stage of their manufacture (to make them fluffy and bind the fibres together)and for their annual washing.
</TRIAL_DESCRIPTION>

<TRIAL_DESCRIPTION>
At the fulling-tub the job has been reduced. The winter rugs and fabrics of the village have been washed and dry to be stored for the following winter. You have worked a lot at the watermill as well and you have proved your worth to the powder miller. When you find him in the raki still, you ask him to employ you. He accepts and tells you to come by tomorrow morning to start. However, as helping hands are always needed in the workshops, he sends you to the tannery to find the tanner and help him.Find the bean in the tannery and scan the QR code of the tool you need for the"fleshing"

<TRIAL>
TRIAL
</TRIAL>
<TRIAL_ID>
19
</TRIAL_ID>
<TRIAL_NAME>
The inner side of the skin
</TRIAL_NAME>
<TRIAL_TYPE>
5
</TRIAL_TYPE>
<TRIAL_DESCRIPTION>
The inner side of the skin has to be cleaned of «flesh» - that is, of nerves, fat and meat remnants. This «flesh» is part of the hypodermis. Once the skins are soft, they are stretched over a beam, after which the tanner scrapes the inner side of the skin with the fleshing knife. This is long curved, almost blunt and double handed, and it has to be used on the surface with care and skill soas not to strain or cut the skin.
</TRIAL_DESCRIPTION>
